Setup Question	= Intel(R) Turbo Boost Technology
Help String	= Turbo Boost automatically allows individual CPU cores to run faster than stock frequency if the processor is operating within power, temperature and current limitations. This can improve performance in single-threaded applications.  Enable =  Turbo Boost will operate at stock settings  Auto = Turbo Boost will operate at stock settings, except when the base clock frequency is altered  Disable = Disables  Turbo Boost. All CPU cores will operate at settings specified by the CPU clock ratio (above). Recommended setting for overclocking.
